Japanese Troops Gather in Taonan 64

▲Assisting Zhang Haipeng's Rebel Army in Attacking North▲Russia Increases Troops Heavily Outside Manchuria

A dispatch from Harbin reports that the Japanese army, on the pretext of repairing the Jiangqiao on the Tao'ang Road,

Page 8

plans to cover Zhang Haipeng's rebel army in another northern invasion. However, because Russian troops have recently continued to increase outside the Manchuria-Sui border, they cannot help but be apprehensive. Currently, the infantry belonging to the Domon of the 2nd Division of the Japanese Army and the Mori company of the Garrison, which have arrived in Taonan, are still stationed in Taonan. According to reports, since the 30th of last month, the 17th Regiment and artillery have been traveling north along the Siping-Taonan Road from Gongzhuling to Taonan. All the employees of the entire Siping-Taonan Road have now been replaced by Japanese. Today, the military agency here received a telegram from Qiqihar stating that the Japanese army is forcing Zhang Haipeng's army to act as the vanguard and attack Longsha. Zhang arrived in Tailai Town on the 31st, but, intimidated by the elite of the Black Army's Wu Brigade and the Reclamation Army, he still hesitates to advance. Russian Consul General Arlohov visited the Japanese Consul General in Harbin, Ohashi Chuichi, yesterday and spoke for a long time. It is reported that the Russian Consul explained the troop deployment on the Manchuria-Sui border, but in the end, he solemnly stated to the Japanese Consul, saying, "Upon the order of my government, I hope to convey to your army that since the Shenyang Incident, the Soviet Union has maintained a bystander attitude and has always adhered to a non-interference policy. Fortunately, the Japanese army has also been able to maintain the rights of a friendly nation and has not advanced into northern Manchuria. However, if the Japanese army advances north in the future, disrupting the traffic order of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Soviet Union will take necessary preventative measures and take appropriate decisive actions." This very clear statement is tantamount to issuing a final warning to the Japanese side. Therefore, there is a rumor that Japanese Consul Ohashi Chuichi will return to Japan to report within a few days. The actions of the Soviet Union in the past two weeks have indeed given Japan serious pause. Japanese Embassy Counselors to Russia Amano Eiji and Teramachi Nobuto secretly returned to Japan to report a few days ago. From this, it should be known that a major upheaval has begun in the Far East situation. The Red Army's 5th Division of the Soviet Union reportedly arrived outside Manchuria on the 31st of last month and was stationed in Daowuli. Special troops such as tank units and signal corps also arrived later. The 3rd Division of the National Defense Army transferred from Chita through Manchuria to Suifenhe. Its air force headquarters moved to Daowuli, and 30 aircraft were stationed at Abagaitu on the border. On the previous day, the Chinese Eastern Railway specially allocated a train of freight cars, about 300 carriages long, to the Manchuria border. Kuznitsov, the Russian Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Harbin, Bershin, the supervisor, and Nigin, the deputy consul, were all recalled to their country on the 31st. At present, there are about 30,000 Russian infantry, artillery, and cavalry outside Manchuria, and about 20,000 outside Suifenhe. Recently, the No. 86 station outside Manchuria was changed to a main station, connecting the Trans-Baikal Railway, in order to facilitate military transportation. Judging from this tense situation, if the Japanese army arbitrarily invades the north, the Russian army will inevitably occupy all parts of the Chinese Eastern Railway. It will be difficult to avoid a war. It is reported that Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of the Black Province, has stated to the Russian Consul in Heiyuan, Mikhailov, that if Zhang Haipeng's rebel army invades the north, it will not be difficult for us to pacify it. There is no need to worry about the Chinese Eastern Railway, and we hope that the Russian side will remain calm and not lightly advance troops, so as not to cause a war in the Far East. On the other hand, Ma has allocated 50,000 yuan to the Tao'ang Road Bureau to repair Jiangqiao within a week, as an excuse for the Japanese army's northward advance. (Evening of November 1st)

Feng Yong Leads a Delegation to Shanghai to Petition 65

▲The Situation of the Petition Delegation Passing Through Tianjin and Jinan

A dispatch from Tianjin reports that Feng Yong, President of Feng Yong University in the Northeast, after escaping to safety in Beiping, believes that the Northeast problem is becoming increasingly serious. Not only has the Japanese army not withdrawn before the 16th of this month, as resolved by the League of Nations, but it has also advanced and tried to invade the Black Province. The situation is critical. Yesterday, he led a Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Delegation of more than 600 people from Beiping to Beijing and Shanghai to petition the peace conference to quickly unite and jointly oppose foreign aggression. The train arrived at Tianjin Station at 11:15 PM. I met Mr. Feng in the car. According to the discussion, the national crisis is now urgent, and if internal unity is not achieved soon, it is equivalent to hastening our own destruction. The people of the Northeast have suffered especially deeply. Therefore, this morning, students from various universities and people's organizations who have fled from the Northeast to Beiping decided to organize a petition delegation and elected me as the commander-in-chief to go to Beijing and Shanghai to request the peace conference representatives to complete cooperation as soon as possible and jointly oppose Japan. When gathering in Beiping, Deputy Commander Zhang sent Deputy Officer Tang Guozhen to dissuade them from going south temporarily, but the students were determined to set off and persisted firmly. Then, they negotiated with Gao Jiyi, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, for vehicles. Gao declined, saying that there were no empty cars. Fortunately, the Pingpu No. 201 train departed from Beiping at 5:20 PM. The crowd decided to temporarily use this train to go south. The students went to the front of the train track to block the train from leaving, and the passengers, appreciating the patriotic enthusiasm of the delegation, voluntarily got off the train to give up their seats. This delegation's trip south is determined to achieve its goals, and any sacrifice will not be spared, etc. After Feng arrived in Tianjin, he telegraphed Deputy Commander Zhang from the Tianjin Station, reporting the purpose of the petition to the south. The original text said, "Beiping Deputy Commander Zhang Junjian, Yong has been publicly elected as the commander-in-chief. The national crisis and hometown hatred cannot be refused. I hastily took office without bidding farewell, vowing to use my remaining body and humble life to fight for a glimmer of hope for my hometown, and to use my loyal heart to protect the righteousness of the country. After arriving in Beijing and Shanghai, I will report in detail. Your brother Feng Yong humbly kowtows." Then, Mr. Feng met with representatives of the Tianjin-based Northeast Refugee Students Delegation and the Japan-returned Student Delegation at the station and had a somber conversation for about an hour. Mayor Zhang Xueming also personally went to the station to meet Feng and invited the students to talk at the station, saying, "Before you gentlemen set off in Beiping, I received a telegram from Deputy Commander Zhang, instructing me to persuade you if your delegation passes through Tianjin. Now that you gentlemen are determined, I have nothing else to say. However, the only hope for this trip south is to take care of your health. Because the climate in the north and south is different, coupled with the anxiety of worrying about the country, please take care of yourselves for the sake of the country. Because my position is different, there are some things I want to say but cannot say. I only hope that we understand each other," etc. It is reported that the delegation's organization is divided into eleven teams, and each team is divided into groups. There is a captain for each team and a leader for each group. There are also sections for secretary, propaganda, negotiation, health affairs, and command, each responsible for its own affairs. The second team of the delegation is the Feng Yong University Volunteer Army, consisting of more than 100 men and women, all in military uniform, carrying white blankets on their backs, looking like an army. When passing through Tianjin, 50 more Northeast students requested to join the trip south. After Mr. Feng approved, the Beining Railway Bureau specially prepared two carriages to be attached to the train. The passengers who purchased tickets to Pukou along the line at the Tianjin Station last night returned all but a few foreigners' tickets and switched to today's train. The detachment required time to reattach carriages in Tianjin, only departing at 1:40 AM this morning. (November 6th)

A dispatch from Jinan reports that the Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Delegation passed through Jinan on its way to Shanghai to petition the peace conference. Our city received a telegram last night, and Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie immediately led officials above the section chief level and Police Bureau Chief Wang Kairu to the station to take care of things and prepared more than 500 catties of steamed buns and thin porridge to be used for entertaining. The Jinan Station received a telegram in advance and immediately notified that no tickets for the Pingpu train would be sold today. The train was originally scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 9:00 AM this morning, but it was delayed by 3 hours and 40 minutes in Beiping last night, so it only arrived at 12:20 PM. Slogans were pasted all over the train. Fengda and the Northeast universities and middle schools' volunteer army were distributed on both sides of the train to maintain order. Fengda's male and female students were wearing military uniforms and blue cloth shoes, all militarized. The female students wore military uniforms and pistols, walked swiftly, and were especially distinctive. The students from other schools were also wearing gray uniforms, with a tragic air and a serious look, and the order was in good shape. Then, the Director of Public Relations, Wang Huayi, and the Commander-in-Chief, Feng Yong, got off the train and spoke with Mayor Wen, Bureau Chief Wang, and newspaper reporters separately. Wang Huayi said that the purpose of the Northeast Petition Delegation's trip to the Shanghai Peace Conference, not to Nanjing, is because the situation in the Northeast is so serious that tens of millions of people have fallen into the abyss. The key to survival is imminent, but the Shanghai conference has not yet reached an agreement, and there is still no consensus on external affairs. How can the Northeast be rescued? There are three purposes for this trip: (1) to promote the completion of the peace conference, (2) to immediately realize a unified government, and (3) to urge the Party and state officials to eliminate their prejudices and determine a foreign policy. As for the organizational aspect, there are a total of twelve teams, each with ten groups, and each group with ten people, for a total of 1,200 people. The highest-level cadres are the command department, with twelve commanders and one commander-in-chief, which Mr. Feng Yong will serve. The affairs are divided into six groups: public relations, propaganda, affairs, health, supervision, and secretariat. The participants are all from the Northeast, mostly students, as well as representatives from various agencies and organizations, and farmers, workers, and merchants. There are more than 100 women. This trip will only return if the Shanghai conference succeeds and hopes to reach an agreement before the 16th to jointly oppose foreign aggression and achieve Japan's goal of withdrawing troops on the 16th. It is impossible to rely on the League of Nations alone now. A unified government must be established before diplomacy can be carried out. Before departing from Beiping, we experienced many difficulties. We originally planned to board the train at 5:00 PM yesterday, but the Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, Gao Jiyi, refused to attach the carriages, so it did not happen. Then, after the delegation expressed that it was determined to go south no matter what, Deputy Commander Zhang first sent Deputy Officer Tang to dissuade us, and then sent Zhang Zuoxiang and Wang Shuhan to persuade us and invited us to talk at the Prince Shuncheng's mansion, which was unanimously rejected. We arrived at the station at 8:00 PM and asked the Chinese people who had already boarded the train to give up their seats so that everyone could go south. The foreigners on the train were not moved. When we arrived in Tianjin, we received food from the authorities and much help from the press. On this trip to Shanghai, we stand on the national position, not leaning towards one faction or attacking another, only urging the Party and state officials to complete the peace conference and relieve the suffering of the people in the Northeast. If the peace conference is not successful, we will die in Shanghai and not return, etc. Next, Feng Yong said that the situation in the Northeast is roughly as reported in the newspapers. The views I advocated have been detailed in previous telegrams, and I stand on the national position and sacrifice myself for the country. I plan to visit Chairman Chiang in Beijing and urge the Party and state leaders to sacrifice their prejudices and complete the peace conference to decide on a foreign policy. When we departed from Beiping yesterday, Deputy Commander Zhang sent people to persuade us, but because the people were excited, we could not stop. Now, most Chinese people are numb, knowing only their families and not their country. I hope that the press will do its best to awaken the Chinese people from their dreams. I have always admired Chairman Han for his frugality and hard work. China's production is very low. If we do not promote thrift, the economy will be in danger in the future. It is regrettable that I could not meet Chairman Han because he was out holding officer training, etc. The train started south at 1:10 PM. (6th)

Lu Province Government Decides to Dredge the Southern Grand Canal 66

▲ Dispatching Personnel to Negotiate with Various Parties for Implementation ▲ Requesting Central Government to Allocate Disaster Relief Bonds

Jinan Correspondence: Among the water disasters in Shandong, the Yellow River is the most serious, but the Southern Grand Canal's inability to discharge water has an even greater impact on the Yellow River's disasters. The Shandong Construction Department has established a Grand Canal Engineering Bureau to dredge the Southern Grand Canal. This year, the Grand Canal Engineering Bureau has been engaged in surveying and mapping, which has long been completed. The second step is how to proceed with dredging. The Construction Department believes that dredging the Southern Grand Canal requires considerable prior consultation with the Huai River Conservancy Commission and the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Recently, Kong Lingrong, Director of the Grand Canal Engineering Bureau, was specially dispatched to Nanjing to carry out this matter. On the one hand, he will also study the mutual relationship in construction works with the Huai River Conservancy Commission and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, so as to avoid temporary barriers or delays in implementation. Mr. Kong has not yet returned to Jinan. The Construction Department believes that dredging the Southern Grand Canal is imperative. This year's Shandong floods are particularly severe, especially in the counties along the Southern Grand Canal. For the purpose of relieving disaster victims, benefiting the people, and eliminating harm, all should be actively carried out. However, due to the large scale of the project and the huge amount of funds required, the Shandong provincial treasury has no such capacity. At today's provincial government standing committee meeting, the Construction Department proposed that the provincial government telegraph the Central Government's Disaster Relief Committee to allocate four million yuan in disaster relief bonds, to be sold on behalf of the province. The funds received will be used for work relief to dredge the Southern Grand Canal. The proposal was approved by the provincial government. The original text of the proposal is recorded below: "It is found that the water disaster in Lu Province this year is extremely serious, and the most severely affected are the counties near the Southern Grand Canal. This Department is responsible for construction and has repeatedly advocated dredging the Southern Grand Canal and lakes. Recently, in view of the tragedy of this year's water disaster, it is even more felt that this project is an urgent plan for water conservancy construction. However, after this major disaster, with the suffering population everywhere, it is really difficult to mobilize the people to start construction. It is heard that the Central Government's Disaster Relief Committee is issuing disaster relief bonds and distributing them to various provinces to save disaster victims throughout the country. If the Southern Grand Canal project can obtain this funding, then the start of construction will be easier to proceed. It is proposed that the county government forward a telegram to the Central Government's Disaster Relief Committee on the situation of the Lu Canal awaiting treatment, requesting the allocation of four million yuan in disaster relief bonds to be sold on behalf of this province. The funds received will be used to implement work relief and dredge the Southern Grand Canal, which can not only relieve disaster victims but also eliminate floods, achieving both goals with one action. The matter is feasible. This proposal is hereby submitted for public decision." (November 6th)

Jiangsu People Request a Prohibition on Reclamation of Reed Marshes in Luzhou 67

▲Preserving Reeds to Protect Dikes▲Luzhou is Not Suitable for Reclamation

Wei Jiahua, Su Minsheng, Huang Yuexuan, Jiang Zhongxiang, Yang Ziyuan and others, permanent members of the Jiangning Water Disaster Relief Association, presented a petition to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating: "We humbly believe that the cause of natural disasters lies in human actions. The fundamental way to defend against disasters is to cultivate and protect. Since the establishment of this Association, it has been more than a month. It gathers the spirit of gentry, merchants, and organizations, and fulfills the responsibilities of the local community. Jiangning County, along the river, has reported sinking disasters everywhere. Among them, there are countless large and small dikes that have collapsed and been submerged. The members of this Association have repeatedly gone to the disaster areas to investigate the actual situation. It is roughly estimated that the loss of farmland is more than 630,000 mu, and the number of people affected by the disaster is more than 200,000. The disaster situation in the areas of the sandbar north and south dikes and Daizi Island is particularly serious. Just taking the largest sandbar dike breach as an example, it is nearly two hundred and several tens of zhang, which is truly an unprecedented catastrophe in our Ning. The cause of this is not only the high water level this time, but also the lack of flood prevention efforts at ordinary times. Dikes are for flood prevention, and the reeds outside the dikes are for protecting the dikes. In recent years, people have been misled by private gains and officials have been biased towards the benefits of reclamation. They have spared no effort to cut down and destroy the reed marshes that have protected the dikes for thousands of years, turning them into wheat fields. Although they may still pay reed taxes, they have actually become wheat fields. How much is the profit from the harvest? But once the reed beaches are gone, the shielding is completely lost. The wind and water are becoming more and more turbulent, and the dike foundations are becoming more and more loose. In the event of a year of heavy floods, it will inevitably become a swamp. If a prohibition is not imposed quickly, then the wheat fields that are currently planted will be the reclaimed land that will be released in the future. As the ancients said, 'competing with water for land,' now we are going a step further and saying, 'removing reeds to plant wheat,' which is no different from digging our own fences, drinking poisonous wine to quench our thirst. The national economy is at stake, and the people's livelihood is at stake. The relative advantages and disadvantages are more than doubled. This is the crux of the problem, which is even more obvious to everyone. The elders of the sandbar dike and Daizi Island areas have repeatedly prostrated themselves, weeping, and reporting together that after the great disaster, repairing the dike is not enough to prevent floods, and planting reeds extensively is not enough to defend the outer dikes. They implore us to forward their requests to the officials and to approve the restriction. From now on, within fifty zhang outside the dikes along the river, reeds must be preserved and reclamation must not be allowed, and this will be a permanent strict prohibition. In this way, hundreds of thousands of people's lives and homes can be guaranteed, and it will also be the ultimate intention of the late Premier to be concerned about people's livelihood, prevent disasters, and provide disaster relief, which will be forever manifested without end. We beg you to review and approve for implementation, and we are waiting for your order with utmost anxiety."

Local Correspondence

Wuxi 68

Ruffians Show Off Ferocity and Go to the Court to Verify Injuries. Gu Chunquan, Gu Chuntang, Jin Agui, Deng Rongbao, Chen Ating and other five ruffians in Qianzhou Town, Fifteenth District (Qingnian City), have been causing trouble for no reason and treating the villagers as fish and meat. Recently, they set up a gambling den on Wangjiatan nearby, calling on gamblers to extract profits. The other day, the chief of the Public Security Fifteenth Sub-bureau patrolled to the place and suddenly heard the sound of cards. He immediately implemented an arrest. As a result, six gamblers, including Jiang Sibao, were arrested and taken to the bureau, fined, and released. However, the boss Gu Chunquan and others believed that this arrest was caused by Shi Aming's report, so they hated him to the bone. They gathered their accomplices and beat Aming severely, causing him to be covered in injuries and lying on the ground, unable to get up. Chunquan and others saw that they had caused trouble and dispersed. After being beaten and injured, Shi Aming, in addition to seeking medical treatment, also came to the city yesterday (8th) to go to the county court procuratorate to verify the injuries and request the arrest of the perpetrators for legal action.

Confiscated Enemy Goods Handled and Appraised. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of various circles in this county held an executive committee meeting at 3 pm yesterday (8th) to resolve cases. One was that the confiscated enemy goods have been identified and confirmed, and Committee Member Xu Hanqing was responsible for handling the appraisal matters in order to implement the matter. One was that Yisheng Silk Store sent a letter requesting lenient punishment, which was difficult to approve. One was that the Yixing County Chamber of Commerce sent a letter requesting that when verifying, non-enemy goods should be stamped with a "Verified" mark so that the goods would not cause further complications when they arrived in Yixing. It was decided that all goods identified and returned would be allowed to be stamped and replied for verification. One was that Xiangyu Silk and Cloth Store was found to have Japanese goods such as velvet after registration and was dealt with according to regulations. One was that Director Shi Qinglin of the Identification Committee and Director Xu Hanqing of the Custody Department reported the results of the identification and were dealt with according to regulations. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Careless Examination and Request for Re-examination. Wu Pu, a rural woman from Wujiali Village, Tu 421, Eleventh District of the county, was previously beaten by her clansman Wu Aer and others. She reported to the procuratorate to verify the injuries. Unexpectedly, almost a month later, Pu suddenly died. Her daughter-in-law, Wu Li, reported to the court for an autopsy. Prosecutor Du went to the countryside on the 4th of this month to conduct an autopsy on file. Last night, Wu Li filed a petition with the procuratorate requesting the dispatch of personnel for a re-examination, and pointed out that the previous autopsy was careless. I wonder how Chief Zhou will handle it.

Changzhou 69

Killing a Notorious Bandit Yichi Tou, a notorious bandit in Beixiang, Wuyi County (namely Qi Renfu), has been wanted by the county government for a long time, but has not been arrested. The bandit recently gathered his accomplices to hold a meeting at Caojiaba near Baizhang Town in the Fourth District, secretly plotting wrongdoing. The matter was detected by Chen Tianxi, captain of the Second Police Squad, who immediately dispatched Squad Leader Guo to lead the police to surround Caojiaba on the 7th. As expected, bandits came out to resist arrest. Yichi Tou fired a gun. After the police team returned fire, Yichi Tou was shot in the head and chest and immediately fell to the ground and died. A White Langlin pistol was found on his body, and eight of his accomplices were captured and secretly taken to Guotangqiao Town for further reporting to the county government and county court for verification.

A Kidnapping Case Occurred in the Fourth District. Several bandits suddenly came to the home of Rui Fusheng in Huaiyong Township, Fourth District, Wuyi County, the other night, climbed over the wall and entered the room, kidnapped Rui Fusheng, and went north over the railway.

Zhang Qian's Property Actually Returned. The arrest warrant for Zhang Qian in this county has been cancelled. All the properties that have been sealed in Nantong and Dongtai are now being returned. The county government received an instruction from the Department of Civil Affairs, saying, "In order to obey orders, in the case of Zhang Qian in Nantong, the Executive Yuan has now issued an instruction to cancel the arrest warrant. The original case of confiscation of property as decided by the 57th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee should be revoked accordingly. In addition to ordering the Department of Education to be informed, the Department is hereby ordered to forward it to the county magistrate for compliance, return the previously sealed property of Zhang Qian, obtain a receipt, and submit a detailed inventory for inspection and transfer without any delay."

Zhenjiang 71

Sanheba Has a Dike Built. Sanheba is the throat of the Huai River's return to the Yangtze River. The Construction Department previously telegraphed the Huai River Conservancy Commission to build a dike. It is now heard that the Anhui Construction Department has appointed Wu Jichun to go to Sanheba to strictly urge the construction of the dike. The right to manage the dike has been striven for by the Jiangsu provincial water conservancy authorities for many years without achieving their goal. The authority is not in their hands, so the opening and closing cannot be done on time. This is also a major problem in Jiangsu's water conservancy.

Recent Situation of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Huanhu Road Project. The Huanhu Road runs from Yixing through Wuxi, Wu County, Wujiang, and directly to Nanxun Town on the Zhejiang border, with a total length of 205 kilometers. The Xixun section is about 146 li long (the estimated cost of the entire section is about 2 million yuan). The Xiyi section is about 59 kilometers long. The earth base of the Xiyi section and part of the Xixun section has been built for about 84 kilometers in total. There are a total of 181 bridges and 535 culverts on the entire Huanhu Road. The counties through which the route passes have successively built 55 completed bridges and 210 culverts. The former director of the road, Yu Heng, was transferred to the blocking work and could not take care of both. He has now been replaced by Yu Wei, the director of the Shijuyi section of the Provincial Juyi Road, who was transferred from the department.

Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Extended to Jiangyin. The Jiangsu provincial long-distance telephone was initially used for calls between Zhenjiang, Jurong, Lishui and other nine counties in the nineteenth year. Wuxi and Suzhou were connected in January of the twentieth year. Changshu was connected this month. Now, the telephone has been extended to Jiangyin. The line runs from the Wuxi exchange to the north and west, passing through Qinxiang and Qingyang to reach Jiangyin County, which is about 80 li long. The project is estimated to cost about 16,630 yuan. The funds were allocated by the Construction Bonds Supervision and Use Committee under the long-distance telephone fee item. The management of long-distance telephones used to belong to the Electrical Management Office, but now the office has been abolished and changed to the Fourth Section of the Construction Department. It is heard that the materials needed for the Jiangyin line have been prepared, the team leader is Li Xia, and the entire team has more than 40 employees. They will set off soon to start laying the line.

Qingjiang 72

Director Zhu Dismissed and Investigated. The director of Huaiyin Public Security Bureau, Zhu Ying, was discovered by Chief Liang to have had his bureau members, Yuan Xuepu, induce the purchase of firearms from the garrison. He was telegraphed to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Pacification Superintendent's Office of this province. The county was also instructed to place Zhu under supervision. It has been ten days since the incident. Now, Inspector Wu Xie from the Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs was specially dispatched to Pubei to investigate the matter. Wu arrived in Pu on the 3rd and first went to the county government to investigate everything. According to his words to others, the department had already dismissed Zhu and ordered him to await investigation. Shen Shi has been appointed as the acting director of Huaiyin Public Security Bureau and is expected to arrive in Huaiyin to take over the matter around the 6th.

The Ending of the Three Industries' Market Stoppage. The cloth, general merchandise, and miscellaneous goods industries in Huaiyin stopped the market due to the stagnation of finance. After the party and government mediated, the market reopened on the 2nd of this month after a delay of five days. However, regarding the method of activating finance, there was a saying of mortgaging Japanese goods to various Qian Zhuang (money shops), so yesterday (3rd) at 3 pm, County Chief He, Party Secretary Qian, Chamber of Commerce Standing Committee Member Dai, and representatives of the three industries, Wu Ganqing, Meng Zizhang, Mao Shaoping, Chen Yanling, Qian Industry Guild Standing Committee Member Zhang Runsheng and others, discussed the matter at the county government. As a result, the cloth industry borrowed 60,000 yuan, the general merchandise industry borrowed 5,000 yuan, and the miscellaneous goods industry borrowed 5,000 yuan. Each mediator provided a guarantee for a period of 50 days with a monthly interest rate of 1.3%. The loan agreement was agreed upon.

All refugees in various places will stop being accommodated. If your county has refugees, please do not send them again to avoid repeated transfers."

Hangzhou 74

Measures to Eliminate Bandits on the Borders of Three Provinces. Zhejiang, Jiangsu, and Anhui provinces are located adjacent to each other. All bandits on the borders easily evade thorough resolution due to the provincial boundary relationship by fleeing from one to the other. Recently, the Changxing Coal Mine Bureau was robbed, and bandits from Jiangxi Province invaded Huabu in Zhejiang Province on a large scale. It is not possible to be successful unless the three provinces jointly suppress them. The Zhejiang Provincial Government received a telegram from the headquarters yesterday, specially appointing Li Mingyang, director of the Security Office of Jiangsu Province, as the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in the three provinces, and Zhang Yineng, commander of the Fourth Regiment, as the commander of bandit suppression in the Liyang Yixing area. Shen Guocheng, commander of the Seventh Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Brigade, will concurrently serve as the commander of bandit suppression in the Changxing Anji area, and Xu Guoting, commander of the Anhui Provincial Security Brigade, will concurrently serve as the commander of bandit suppression in the Guangde Jianping area. All bandit suppression matters in the three provinces will be fully commanded by Li Mingyang, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression. All bandit gangs on the borders of Zhejiang, Jiangsu, and Anhui provinces must be completely eliminated within one month to maintain the safety of the people.

Shangyu 75

A Kidnapping Case Occurred in Dongxiang. Bao Jiahai's home outside the Nanchang Bridge in Baocun, Dongxiang, seven li from the county seat, was broken into by eight bandits holding wooden shell guns at around 4 pm on the 4th. They attempted to kidnap his nephew Yuanjin, but were unsuccessful. Shao Feizi Submits a Detailed Report to the Ministry on the Zhejiang University Turmoil 76

▲ Li Ximou Requests to Resign Due to Improper Supervision ▲ Zhao Zhiyou Visits the President and is in Mediation

Shao Feizi, president of National Zhejiang University, resigned from the Ministry of Education on the same day after a conflict with students of the Engineering College who petitioned for the issuance of military training fees. He was quickly dispatched to replace him. Yesterday, he submitted a detailed report to the Ministry of Education. Now, Li Ximou, president of the Engineering College, has also requested to resign due to self-reproach. The affairs of the college are handled by Li Shouheng, director of academic affairs. Professors of the Engineering College sent a letter requesting the president to abandon his intention to resign. It is also heard that Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou volunteered to serve as a mediator. The text of Shao Feizi's report to the Ministry is recorded as follows: (Omitted above) In the middle of last month, Tan Xihong, Dean of the College of Agriculture of this university, sent a letter requesting to resign. His intention was extremely firm. Although the president and the faculty and staff of the College of Agriculture repeatedly and earnestly tried to persuade him to return to the college, he did not agree. The president believed that the affairs of the school could not be stopped for a day, so he immediately discussed with Xu Xuan, the former director of academic affairs of the college, to succeed as the dean, and invited the directors of the various departments of the college and the directors of the agricultural, forestry, and horticulture fields, as well as the associate professors in the college, to organize the college affairs committee to temporarily maintain the situation before the new dean arrived. Since the establishment of the committee, the funding issues of the college have been discussed by the committee members and handled by the president at any time. Currently, the funding of this university has not been received for January and February of this year, and the allocation from Zhejiang Province has not been received in full for June, and only 10,000 yuan was received in September. The difficult situation is beyond words. The students of the College of Agriculture, believing that the college affairs committee could not be directly responsible for the funding, came to request instructions on the afternoon of the 4th of this month. The president immediately summoned the students to talk in the auditorium. (Omitted in the middle) While explaining, students from the First and Second Battalions of the Engineering College Student Volunteer Army suddenly entered the meeting place. At first, they were sitting in the audience. Later, the president temporarily left the meeting due to some matter and talked with the professors of the College of Agriculture. Several students from the Engineering College also left the meeting and came to request a separate conversation with the president. The president immediately allowed them. At that time, the professors of the College of Agriculture did not hear the president's reply to the students. They instructed the students to talk to the president after the students of the College of Agriculture had left, but the students said that the professors of the College of Agriculture should not interfere. They then used the organization of the Student Volunteer Army to request the battalion commander to immediately expel the professors of the College of Agriculture, and said not to let the president escape. The president was angry at the students' deliberate insult to the teachers, and scolded them. The students immediately shouted and attacked. The students of the college in the venue also swarmed in. The president and Dean Li of the Engineering College were unable to stop them. The president was then crowded into the office by several professors of the College of Agriculture, hoping that the students would regain their reason and then guide them. However, the students surrounded the office again and sent a team to guard the telephone, as if facing a major enemy. They supported Dean Li and prevented him from interfering. Then the students broke the glass bolt of the office door and rushed in to reason with the president. It was obvious that they intended to stir up trouble. At this point, the president knew that it was impossible to reason with them and that it was impossible to maintain the situation any longer, so he immediately announced his resignation. The students then deliberated for a long time before shouting slogans and retreating. This is the actual situation of the turmoil. Omitted below.

Various Schools Add Extra Lectures on the History of Japanese Aggression Against China 77

The Ministry of Education approved the letter from the Central Training Department, stating that schools at all levels should add temporary extracurricular lectures for several hours each week, specifically lecturing on the history of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China. In addition to notifying the national colleges and universities above the specialist level and the Weihaiwei Management Office, it also ordered the education halls and bureaus of each province and city to say, "The Central Executive Committee Training Department's letter No. 18097 opened, 'Since the September 18th Incident in the three northeastern provinces, the executive committees of Shanxi Province, Nanjing Special City, etc., and the Jinpu Railway Party Affairs Reorganization Committee have repeatedly submitted suggestions that schools at all levels should add lectures on the history of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China or suspend classes for a week and change the lectures to the causes, current situation, and countermeasures that the people of the country should have for this national humiliation. Japanese imperialism is plotting to invade me and wants to avenge its shame. It is not possible to be successful unless we start with education. However, the curriculum and teaching time of schools at all levels have regulations. If we add courses in the middle, it is inconvenient. In order to meet the current needs, it seems feasible to add temporary extracurricular lectures on the history of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China. However, there is no need to suspend classes for lectures. In addition to replying separately, please inform the schools at all levels under your jurisdiction to follow these instructions.' The Ministry of Education has issued an urgent order to the schools under its jurisdiction to follow these instructions."

Private Elementary School Teachers and Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation Congress 80

On November 8th, teachers and students from all private elementary schools in Shanghai held a joint anti-Japanese national salvation congress at the Public Recreation Ground. Starting from 7 a.m., teachers and students from various elementary schools continuously flocked to the venue, their spirits high and order well-maintained. Over one hundred organizations attended, and representatives from the Municipal Education Bureau and other departments came to provide guidance. There were more than 5,000 attendees. Scouts from schools such as Moore Memorial Church, Shanghai Middle School, Municipal South, De Run, and China Industrial maintained order at the venue. The Public Security Bureau dispatched a large police team to oversee the event. The meeting commenced around 10 a.m. The presidium consisted of representatives from Municipal South, Cheng Zhong, Hui Qun, and Guo Ren. The master of ceremonies was from Shi Guang, the recorder from Shanghai Academy, the general commander from Municipal South, commanders from Hu Nan, De Run, and Ai Qun, and the disciplinary team from Shanghai Junior Xiehe. The reception was handled by Yin Jiang, at the request of Qiang Hua, demonstrating great enthusiasm. First, Song Yuntao from Municipal South reported the purpose of the meeting and the progress of the association, covering (1) the history of Japanese aggression against our country, (2) the fact that private elementary schools did not want to lag behind in anti-Japanese national salvation, hence the organization of this association, and (3) given the urgency of foreign aggression, this congress was specially convened to expand publicity. Next, a representative from the Municipal Education Bureau, Mr. Yang, delivered a speech, followed by speeches from celebrities from various organizations, all of which were heartfelt. Students from Ai Qun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School and other schools gave speeches on stage, their language pure and receiving much applause, which was sufficient to promote the public's determination to resist Japan and save the country. Finally, Cheng Zuxin from Hui Qun read the proposals of the congress, which were unanimously passed, including (1) that this association send a telegram urging the Nanjing-Guangdong sides to cooperate sincerely and quickly save the country (telegram recorded below), (2) requesting the peace conference representatives to quickly decide on a declaration of war against Japan, (3) that private elementary schools unite to organize volunteer troops to go to the country's aid, and (4) implementing a complete economic severance of relations with Japan. After the meeting, there were originally plans for a full parade, but due to the current situation, it was temporarily canceled.

▲Telegram Urging Nanjing-Guangdong Cooperation to Quickly Rescue the Nation. The Republic of China is unfortunate, with disasters and turmoil following one after another for the past twenty years. Tracing the origin of the disaster, it is actually due to the failure of the advanced members of the party and state to cooperate, which led to this. The Japanese pirates were able to take advantage of the situation, which is painful to speak of. Can they not feel ashamed? Fortunately, both Nanjing and Guangdong sides have jointly awakened and each sent representatives to gather in Shanghai, full of hope for peace and with unification in sight, so the national crisis can be saved. Who knew that after only a few days, various obstacles arose, and discussions were repeatedly suspended? The future is difficult to predict, but the public's anxiety is increasing day by day. This association, in view of the daily worsening of the current situation and the increasing urgency of the brutal Japanese aggression, convened the All-Shanghai Private Elementary School Anti-Japanese National Salvation Congress at the Public Recreation Ground today (November 8th), resolving to send a telegram requesting the Nanjing and Guangdong sides to cooperate sincerely and quickly save the country, and resolving to abide by all resolutions of the peace conference, with no one allowed to undermine them. If anyone comes out to undermine peace or obstruct the progress of the peace conference, this association will do everything in its power, for the sake of the country's future, to deal with them. This is an urgent plea, hoping everyone will work hard for the country. Respectfully submitted by the All-Shanghai Private Elementary School Teachers and Staff Anti-Japanese National Salvation Congress.

Baseball Field Crowded: Tung Wah Eliminates Nanshanbao in Last Minute 89

│Sco-Tu Cup First Week Replay│

▲Dai Linjing's Miraculous Pass│Chen Hongguang's Standard Kick

▲2 to 1 Sets the Outcome│15,000 People Cheer Wildly

The baseball field was crowded. The Tung Wah and Nanshanbao football teams competed in the first week replay of the Sco-Tu Cup yesterday. Tung Wah broke the 0 to 0 tie from the last game. In the last minute, Chen Hongguang scored a goal with a pass from Dai Linjing, eliminating Nanshanbao with a score of 2 to 1, and entering the second week.

▲Tung Wah Team Lineup

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Guan Xun'an, Chen Pu, Tu Kaiyuan, Chen Jiaqiu, Qian Jingyong, Chen Hongguang, Dai Linjing, Li Yishen, Chen Yutian

▲Nanshanbao Team Lineup

Loran, Qi Shi, Huo Luosi, Yi Ai'er, Po Man, Bao En, Yang Ge, Xue Te'er, Fa Weike, Fu Late, Maidison

▲Unprecedented Crowd of 15,000 People

The first Sco-Tu Cup battle between Tung Wah and Nanshanbao ended in a 0 to 0 tie. Therefore, both teams worked hard and practiced even harder, determined to win. When the two heroes met again, the battle was bound to be even fiercer. Therefore, yesterday's spectators were even more numerous than last time, reaching as many as 15,000 people, so that there was no space to stand. Those who were seated also had to stand up. Even women and children stood for ninety minutes. The grand occasion can be imagined.

▲Firecrackers Explode as Athletes Enter

Ten minutes before the start of the game, Tung Wah team captain Zhou Xianyan led the entire army of soldiers to the field to fight. The sound of firecrackers suddenly rose, shaking the sky, wishing Tung Wah victory. The enthusiasm of support was evident. Zhou's red jersey was bright and eye-catching. It was said that red represents joy, which is why Tung Wah protects victory.

▲Tung Wah Forwards Leap Like Dragons and Tigers

Tung Wah's five forwards yesterday were incredibly sharp. Their cooperation in advancing and retreating was smooth and admirable, and their movements were lightning-fast. In the blink of an eye, they had reached the Nanshan army's goal. Unfortunately, they missed countless scoring opportunities. Therefore, amidst the praises, there were also some regrets. Each of the five forwards was active and impeccable. Because of the fierce attack of the forwards, Zhou Xianyan's position was not as tense as last time. Due to the fading performance of Tu Kaiyuan, the center-back line lost this central connection, and the actions before and after felt slightly exhausted.

▲Enemy Goal Shakes Within One Minute

Within one minute of contact, Tung Wah launched a full-line offensive. Tu Kaiyuan sent a long ball, Qian Jingyong dribbled straight in, Chen Hongguang passed it to the center, the center forward Dai chipped it to the right corner, Chen Yutian caught up, Chen Jiaqiu sent another kick, Dai and Li Yishen had already reached the goal. Nanshanbao's goalkeeper desperately defended, but Li Yishen missed a great opportunity, causing a burst of regret to rise from the four sides. At this time, only one minute had passed since the start of the game.

▲A Slanting Fly Causes Tung Wah to Lose Ground

Tu Kaiyuan then sent another ball, Qian Jingyong hooked it up, the landing point was extremely accurate, but it was still not scored. Li Yishen passed the ball to Dai, Chen Jiaqiu sent it to Yutian, Yutian flew forward and stormed in. Chen Hongguang received it and headed it, but the force was too great, and it flew over the bar. Tung Wah's momentum in the first half was extremely strong. Unexpectedly, after a fierce attack for a quarter of an hour without breaking through, Nanshan's general Bao Man intercepted the ball and sent it flying to the left corner. Xue Te'er gently waved it to the left, Yang Ge lifted his foot and shot, powerfully and accurately. The momentum was fierce, Zhou Xianyan was caught off guard, and Tung Wah conceded a goal first.

▲Miraculous Cooperation Leads to Enemy Goal Falling

Tung Wah, unintentionally falling into the enemy's trap, did not lose heart and actively attacked. Three extremely good corner kicks all proved ineffective. Tung Wah's momentum gradually showed signs of fatigue. The Nanshan army then launched an attack. Qian Jingyong was very active on the left. Once he received a ball from the center forward Dai, he was only five yards from the goal, but he hesitated slightly and missed the chance. After half an hour of fighting, Qian received the ball and quickly sent it to Zhou Dai. Chen Yutian passed it inward, Li Yishen, without deviating, shot it into the net. The cooperation was miraculous, reaching its peak. Tung Wah then created a 1 to 1 tie.

▲Great Luck as Penalty Kick Misses

Only five minutes were left before the end of the first half. Suddenly, Chen Jiaqiu violated the rules in the penalty area, and a penalty kick was awarded. The atmosphere was tense, as if a great disaster was imminent. Zhou Xianyan calmly waited for the change. Center forward Fa Weike used his skills and shot up to the upper corner, but the ball flew half an inch too high, grazed the bar, and bounced back to the left. Li Ning hurriedly rescued it. This penalty kick that did not score was Tung Wah's great luck and a sign of victory. The first half ended in a 1 to 1 tie.

▲Second Hit Disallowed Due to Offside

After a five-minute break, they switched sides and fought again. Tung Wah's momentum in the second half was as sharp as before. Qian Jingyong passed the ball to Dai, Luo Shimei missed, the center forward flew the pass to Chen Yutian, Yutian crossed the Shi Huo guard and rushed in like flying, rushed to the goal, and kicked a slanting ball, hitting the enemy's net appropriately. The referee announced that the center forward Dai was offside first, and then Chen Hongguang attacked again, but it was also disallowed due to offside. Those who regretted and resented this were all over the field.

▲Center Forward Ejected, Enemy Army Collapses

With the two disallowed, the two sides remained in a stalemate, with advances and retreats, each missing opportunities. Exhausted and tired, both showed signs of fatigue. Fifteen minutes were left before the end. The Nanshan army advanced to the Tung Wah goal. The referee blew the whistle and ordered them to retreat because the center forward was offside. This center forward, Fa Weike, was very resentful because of the failure of his success. He directly accused the referee of being unreasonable, and his behavior was out of line. The referee immediately ordered him to be sent off the field. With the main general gone, Nanshanbao's offensive power was completely lost. Thus, they collapsed, defending rather than attacking, only hoping to create another tie.

▲Triumph in the Last Minute

With Nanshanbao only defending and not attacking, Tung Wah also showed signs of fatigue. Everyone expected a tie, but who knew that狂欢 [unable to find exact translation but means wild joy/celebration] was there. With only about a minute left, Chen Yutian got the ball from the right, passed through the Shi Huo guard, and immediately whipped the horse. The center forward Dai saw that the opportunity had come and flew up to respond. Chen saw the Shi Huo guard behind him and quickly sent it to Dai. The center forward saw Luo Shimei rushing to block his progress and quickly sent it to the left. Chen Hongguang had already taken the lead. Luo Lan at this point, even if he had three heads and six arms, could only wait to die. Hong kicked it in first. Tung Wah quickly dispatched soldiers to the camp to defend tightly. Then the referee blew the whistle and announced the end. Tung Wah then advanced to the second week with a score of 2 to 1. Firecrackers filled the sky, and they dispersed in wild celebration.

Wang Wu's Speech to Union Representatives 90

▲Detailed Account of the Peace Conference

Yesterday morning, representatives from various labor unions and trade associations, as well as the Revolutionary Workers' Grand Alliance, brought a petition each to Wu's residence at 29 Gordon Road to petition. Because the preparatory meeting had ended the afternoon before yesterday, there was no meeting at Wu's residence yesterday, and the Nanjing and Guangdong representatives did not go either. Only Wang Jingwei and Wu Chaoshu were there. They received the representatives and gave a speech. The list of labor unions and Wang Wu's speech are recorded below:

▲List of Labor Unions: Seamen's Union, Joint Association of Chinese Employees of Customs, Construction Workers' Union, Guangdong Cotton Fluff Industry Union, National Pharmaceutical Industry Union,
