Industry Union, Dingfeng Yarn Tube Union, Xiangchang Yarn Factory Union, China Stock Exchange Union, Wharf Union, Ordnance Factory Union, Railway Mechanical Union.

▲Wang Wu's Speech (1) Wang Jingwei's speech: "Representatives, first I want to explain to everyone that, traditionally, the Nanjing and Guangdong representatives have been meeting here at 9 o'clock every day. Today, because yesterday's meeting has already produced results, the Nanjing representatives did not come today. Only Mr. Wu and I are here. We can give you a general report. Last night, the peace and unity conference reached a conclusion. The representatives of both sides have jointly issued a telegram reporting the process of the resolution. You may not have seen it yet, so let me briefly summarize it again. Everyone knows that the Kuomintang is divided. In the past, why did we want to overthrow the Northern Warlords? It was because the actions of the Northern Warlords violated democratic politics. If the people of the Kuomintang cannot achieve democratic politics, we cannot but work to overthrow them. Otherwise, there is no reason for it. Now all the comrades and the people of the country are suffering deeply. I personally feel the same suffering as the people. Since Japan forcibly occupied the Northeast, the people of the Northeast must be even more painful. The reason is the lack of democratic politics. Originally, the country is like a boat, and the government is just the person steering the boat. In civilized countries, if it is found that the person steering the boat is incompetent, especially in times of great wind and dangerous waves, the people have the right to replace the person steering the boat. The person steering the boat has no choice but to listen. This is the meaning of democratic politics. Recently, Nanjing felt that using soldiers internally was not a good solution. Therefore, it sent Mr. Cai, Zhang, Chen, and others as representatives. The Guangdong Extraordinary Conference also sent me and others as representatives to discuss the reform of party affairs and politics and the foreign policy. The first thing we discussed was the foreign policy. The first thing we decided was to be consistent externally. However, there is an attached explanation to external consistency.

In this incident in the three northeastern provinces, the border troops completely resisted, and how many places were lost in a few hours. This is not consistent. The principle of consistent policy, the Nanjing side also said, if the brutal Japanese come to invade again, we will definitely make a defensive resistance. At the same time, because the National Government in Nanjing is recognized by the international community, it was decided that Nanjing will be responsible for foreign affairs, and the negotiation policy must be jointly determined by everyone. The current approach is to ask the League of Nations to uphold justice. At the same time, we must prepare for the final determination to resist. We understand what the comrades present are enthusiastically demanding. I also have the final determination to resist. The second is the reform of the political system. For the past few years, it has been called tutelage, but in reality, it is military rule. Tutelage is different from enlightened autocracy. Tutelage is to gradually build constitutionalism. The reform of the political system is to advocate the separation of military and civilian affairs. The chairman should not have great power. If the chairman is not good, he should resign. People in civilized countries know that if others are dissatisfied with them, they will leave themselves, and they will never use cannons to bomb before leaving. As for the commander-in-chief, civilized countries do not set it up in peacetime. Even the Japanese Emperor only concurrently serves as the Grand Marshal in wartime. There is no such thing as a Commander-in-Chief of the two capitals with such high power over everything. In short, for the political reform plan, the first point is to amend the Organic Law of the National Government, so the issue of the system can be resolved. The second point is to reorganize the National Government, so the issue of people can also be resolved. Third, regarding financial issues, it was decided to establish a Financial Committee, which would include people's representatives, and give them the power to organize finances, review budgets, audit the issuance of public bonds, audit and report sales, and publish revenue and expenditure accounts. The number of committee members is three from the government and twelve from the people's representatives, so that the people have the right to review finances. The Nanjing representatives also agreed to this point. In the future, unless it is for national defense and bandit suppression, the people should never bear domestic debt. We really understand and sympathize with the burden of the people in the Southeast for the past few years. If public bonds are issued to fight wars, not only will there be no capital, but also the blood and sweat of the people will be sacrificed. If public bonds are issued for construction, then it will naturally be very beneficial. Fourth, regarding all disputes, they should be resolved by a two-thirds majority of the members present at the plenary meeting of the Central Executive Committee and a two-thirds majority of the members present voting anonymously, and not by force. Fifth, regarding party affairs, the issue of the Fourth Plenary Session, Nanjing advocated opening the meeting in Nanjing as scheduled, while Guangdong advocated holding the meeting after the government was reorganized. Now, after negotiation, the Nanjing and Guangdong sides will each hold a meeting in their respective locations. The method of generating candidates will be negotiated by both sides. All diplomatic, political, financial, military, and party proposals will be handled by the First Plenary Session of the Fourth Congress. Now, representatives are being sent back to Nanjing and Guangdong to report and request approval. If both sides approve, then the internal disputes within the party for the past few years can be resolved. I think both sides can probably approve it. If the resolutions negotiated by the two sides this time can be achieved, the separation of military and civilian affairs that you all hope for can be realized. In summary, the demands of the representatives can be divided into political democratization, the military should be solely responsible for bandit suppression and national defense and should not interfere in politics, and the hope for peaceful reunification. You came early, or have not seen the reports in the newspapers, thinking that peace may not be possible, so you came to petition so enthusiastically. Now, peaceful reunification is possible. Please supervise the two sides to abide by the resolutions and further seek true unity and true peace, to resist the aggression of imperialism externally, and to achieve democratic politics internally."

(2) Wu Chaoshu's speech: "Mr. Wang's report has been very clear, and there is no need for me to say more in detail. However, in general, the six of us, as representatives from Guangdong to Shanghai, hold the aim that China's territorial sovereignty cannot be lost in the slightest degree externally, and to establish democratic politics internally. The negotiations at the peace conference also hold the same aim. In the future, we will continue to follow this aim to seek to implement it. Please, Shanghai citizens and the nation, urge us, and please supervise the government to realize it."

After the End of the Peace Preparatory Meeting 91

▲Beijing Representatives Cai, Wu, and Chen Arrived in Beijing Yesterday▲Sun, Chen, and Li Three Representatives Scheduled to Return to Shanghai Tomorrow

The Beijing-Guangdong Peace and Unification Conference was declared concluded the night before last after the seventh preparatory meeting passed a resolution. Yesterday, representatives from various trade associations in Shanghai petitioned both sides. Beijing representatives, except for Zhang Ji who had returned to Nanjing to report, Cai Yuanpei and Wu Tiecheng also went to Beijing yesterday with Chen Mingshu. At the same time, the three Guangdong representatives, Sun Ke, Chen Youren, and Li Wenfan, are scheduled to leave Shanghai tomorrow to return to Guangdong and report to the Extraordinary Congress. The news from yesterday is recorded below:

▲Observations on the Fourth National Congress

Although the Fourth National Congress was decided by the Peace Preparatory Meeting to be held separately, both sides still engaged in the meeting with a spirit of cooperation. According to representatives from both sides, all future national affairs will be resolved by this meeting. After the congress elects the fourth Central Committee members, the committee will produce a unified new government. The political reform plan and other matters decided by the previous Peace Preparatory Meeting will be handled by the fourth Central Executive Committee in the future. As for the election method of the fourth Central Committee members, the total number, including the executive and supervisory committee members and alternate executive and supervisory committee members, is 160 people. Among them, 72 are members of the executive committee, 48 are alternate members of the executive committee, 30 are supervisory committee members, and 20 are alternate supervisory committee members. The results of the review of the qualifications of past committee members by the Preparatory Meeting the day before yesterday, excluding those suspected of communism who have already been expelled from the party, amount to about 112 people. The election in the future will be based on this number, and the remaining 48 people will be selected by Beijing and Guangdong, 24 from each side. After mutual recognition by both sides, a formal decision can be made.

▲Cai, Wu, and Others Have Returned to Beijing

The day before yesterday (7th) afternoon, the seventh preparatory meeting of the Peace Conference appointed Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, and Wu Tiecheng to go to Beijing, and Sun Ke, Chen Youren, and Li Wenfan to go to Guangdong, to report on the progress of the conference and implement the resolutions. Of the three Nanjing representatives, Zhang Ji had already entered Beijing the night before last (7th), Cai Yuanpei took a fast train to Beijing at 9:30 yesterday morning, and Wu Tiecheng and Chen Mingshu took a night express train to Beijing at 11:45 last night to report.

▲Guangdong Representatives Leave Shanghai Tomorrow

The three Guangdong representatives will briefly pack their bags in Shanghai and are scheduled to take the Asian Queen ship to Hong Kong tomorrow (10th), then transfer to Guangzhou. In addition to the attendants of the three representatives, some staff of the Guangdong National Government and a portion of the representatives attending the Fourth National Congress of Guangdong will also travel south on the same ship. The journey is expected to take twelve days to arrive in Hong Kong. Sun, Chen, Li, and others will stay in Guangdong for about ten days, then return to Shanghai and go to Beijing with the dignitaries remaining in Shanghai.

More Than Two Hundred and Sixty Associations Held Important Meetings Yesterday 92

▲Petition Beijing and Guangdong Representatives for Peace▲Telegraph Black Province Chairman to Continue Fighting

Shanghai News reports that more than one hundred and sixty trade associations in Shanghai, including the silk industry, mineral ash industry, lime distribution industry, mercerized cotton weaving industry, north-south goods exchange industry, southern goods industry, and sausage industry, held a meeting yesterday morning. They appointed more than one hundred representatives, including Luo Qinghua, Zheng Chenghua, Ma Shaoquan, Ye Jiaxing, and Zhu Wenqi, to visit the Beijing and Guangdong representatives and petition for peace. They first went to Wu's residence on Gordon Road, where they were received by Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaochu, and Zou Haibin. Luo Qinghua and others first presented their petition, stating that today, we represent more than one hundred and sixty trade associations in Shanghai, petitioning all of you peace representatives to quickly unite sincerely and determine a major plan to secure the country internally and resist foreign aggression. Since the violent Japanese occupied our northeastern regions, the whole country is in panic, and everyone believes that disaster is imminent. If the whole country does not unite to deal with it together, the tragic consequences of the country's demise will be far more than a simple change of dynasties like the Song and Ming. Since the advanced party-state leaders from Beijing and Guangdong came to Shanghai to discuss national affairs, the Shanghai business community felt that our country still had a glimmer of hope. However, half a month has passed without any agreement, and rumors that the two sides may break down at any time have made people even more confused, and the social economy is becoming more dangerous. Shanghai is the central region of the country's industry and commerce. If Shanghai merchants are in this dangerous situation, if the political situation is not stable, they will not be able to support it. If Shanghai's industry and commerce declare bankruptcy, the national economy will inevitably collapse. Even if the violent Japanese do not destroy us, we will destroy ourselves. Shanghai merchants are not afraid of bankruptcy, nor are they afraid of sacrificing their lives, but they ask all the advanced leaders to abandon their prejudices and unite to lead the people to save the country together, so that Shanghai merchants will go bankrupt and sacrifice themselves for the sake of resisting Japan. Otherwise, if the available popular sentiment is not used, and the good nation is allowed to become slaves to a foreign country, then Shanghai merchants really do not know where to die. Now, reading the newspaper, we know that there is already a solution for peace, and we are very happy. However, we hope to realize unification immediately, and that unification cannot be destroyed permanently in the future. All Shanghai merchants respectfully request all of you advanced party-state leaders with twelve thousand points of sincerity, holding the principle that the past cannot be advised, but the future can be pursued, leading the people of the whole country, with the determination to thoroughly correct past mistakes and strive to uplift themselves, to devote themselves to the following requests: (1) Complete peaceful unification immediately and seek sincere unity together; (2) Properly plan for the major policy toward Japan and recover the occupied territory; (3) Cultivate internal administration and thoroughly implement the Three Principles of the People. Now that the national crisis is imminent and time is urgent, merchants dare not clutter the ears with trivial matters. Please base yourselves on the principle of treating the symptoms in an emergency and quickly determine a way to save the emergency. In the future, the reform of all administrations, Shanghai merchants swear to follow you all and work together. We hope that all representatives will give as much guidance as possible. Then Wang responded, stating that the opinions presented will be fully accepted by the representatives. The Nanjing government is responsible for negotiations on foreign issues, because the Nanjing government is the internationally recognized government, and all principles are decided by the meeting, which can be said to be completely consistent. Internal issues will be resolved by the Fourth National Congress held simultaneously in Beijing and Guangdong, electing the fourth Central Executive Committee members. Once approved by the central party headquarters of both sides, it can be implemented. The representatives considered it satisfactory and then went to Wu Tiecheng's residence on Haig Road. Luo Qinghua and others presented the petition to Wu, and Wu, in addition to responding to each item, also stated that he would go to Beijing tonight and contribute your wishes to the central government. The representatives bid farewell and returned, immediately reporting the petition process to the representatives of various associations in the city, and resolved many important cases: (1) Publish a declaration to support peaceful unification and determine a major plan for resisting Japan; (2) Telegraph the chairman of Black Province to encourage Ma Zhanshan to continue fighting; (3) Telegraph Zhang Xueliang, the vice commander, to quickly restore the lost territory. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM.

Wang Bailing, Director of the Volunteer Army Training, Took Office Yesterday 93

▲More Than a Thousand People Attended

Wang Bailing, appointed by the Central Training Directorate as the director of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Army Training Office, held a swearing-in ceremony at Labor University in Jiangwan at 9:00 AM yesterday. Zhang Qun, sent by the Central Government, and Tao Baichuan, sent by the Municipal Party Department, served as oath supervisors. Several hundred guests, including Chu Minyi, Pan Gongzhan, and Zhang Daofan, and more than a thousand representatives from the Volunteer Army of major middle schools attended. The ceremony was quite grand, and the atmosphere was solemn and tragic. The details are as follows:

▲A Glimpse of the Auditorium The auditorium was located at Labor University, surrounded by five-color flags, and the Party and National flags hung high at the door, fluttering in the wind. The entrance was the signing area. Chrysanthemums were placed in front of the swearing-in platform, along with silver shields presented by Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, and various circles. Zhu Yiming, the chief of the General Affairs Section, was in charge of all matters. Zhu Sanwen, Li Yongzhong, Hu Yazhou, Gong Weidao, and Lu Jingzhi served as greeters. The order was excellent, the entire venue was silent, and in the silence, there was a tragic and desolate atmosphere.

▲Attendees Yesterday, in addition to the Central Representative Zhang Qun, the Municipal Party Department Representative Tao Baichuan, and the two oath supervisors, there were also Central Committee Member Chu Minyi, Zhejiang Provincial Party Committee Member Zhang Daofan, General Headquarters Councilor Fan Zhengbo, Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng, Social Affairs Bureau Chief Pan Gongzhan, Education Bureau Chief Xu Peihuang, Arsenal Director Song Shimao, Labor University President Wang Jingqi, Jiaotong University President Li Zhaohuan, Shanghai University President Liu Zhanen, Law School Dean Chu Fucheng, Cultural Academy Li Peitian, Women's Relief Association Lin Kecong, Shanghai Volunteer Army Committee Members Li Cishan and Zhou Yanan, Special Zone District Court Representative Ju Zhijing, Second Special Zone District Court Representative Zhang Yong, District Court Representative Yao Yuanding, and several hundred others. The schools participating in the Volunteer Army included Jiaotong, Law and Politics, Fudan, Aurora, Zhongda, Business School, Law School, Daxia, Jinan, Chizhi, Datong, Shanghai, National Institute of Technology, Sino-French Institute of Technology, Wusong Merchant Marine, Minli, Shibei, Fisheries, Nanyang, Southeast Women's Physical Education, Renhe Midwifery, Qingxin, Huahua, Pudong, Zhengfeng, East Asia Physical Education, Xinmin, Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Huiling, Chengzhong, Liangjiang, and Wuben, among more than eighty schools, with approximately one thousand male and female volunteers.

▲Ceremony Procedure (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respects to the portrait of the Premier; (4) Read the Premier's will; (5) Oath supervisors take their positions; (6) Swearing-in members take their positions; (7) Swearing-in members take the oath; (8) Oath supervisors deliver instructions; (9) Guest representatives deliver speeches; (10) Training director delivers a response; (11) Ceremony concludes; (12) Photography.

▲Swearing-in Situation At 9:30 AM, the swearing-in ceremony began. After the military music played, Wang Bailing and the swearing-in members took their positions simultaneously and took the oath. The oath was as follows: "I swear with utmost sincerity to abide by the Premier's instructions, obey the orders of my superiors, be loyal to my duties, and defend the country. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This is my oath." Then the oath supervisors Zhang Qun and Tao Baichuan and guests Chu Minyi, Lin Kecong, and Li Zhaohuan delivered speeches (record follows). Finally, Wang delivered a response, and the meeting dispersed after photography.

▲Zhang Qun's Speech The Central Representative Zhang Qun delivered a speech, stating that today is the day Mr. Wang Bailing takes office as the director of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Army Training Office. On behalf of the Central Government, I am honored to be present at this grand occasion. The Central Propaganda Department also sent a telegram to me, stating that due to time constraints, they could not come and appointed me to serve as their representative, which I find very honored and joyful. Director Wang has a deep relationship with the past and revolutionary history, having gone to the Huangpu Military Academy to work hard on school affairs with Chairman Chiang, and has made a significant contribution to China's military reform, which is something we greatly admire. I and Mr. Wang have been good friends. Twenty-five years ago, when we were studying in Japan, we joined the Tongmenghui together and worked hard on our studies. At that time, I had a deep understanding of Mr. Wang. Mr. Wang has one thing in particular that is worth emulating, that is, he can conduct in-depth research on anything and achieve great success. This time, the Japanese army invaded Liaoning and Jilin, seizing our land and killing our compatriots. The national situation is at a critical juncture. Our Shanghai students have formed the Youth Volunteer Army organization. The Volunteer Army regulations were issued by the Central Training Directorate, the General Headquarters, and the Ministry of Military Affairs. Since Shanghai is strategically important and has the largest number of students, it is necessary to establish a training office. Therefore, Director Wang was sent to Shanghai to organize the training office. Mr. Wang is not only proficient in military studies but is also a backbone member of our party. Therefore, it is expected that Director Wang's training of the Youth Volunteer Army will be disciplined and scientific in terms of military and education, and will achieve great results. I am also a military man and feel that military training is different from other knowledge. Other knowledge can be studied individually, but military training must be of one mind, observe order, and abide by discipline in order to achieve good results. This is a public group life. Now that the country has reached such a state, we must sleep on our weapons and defend against Japan, and go to the national crisis together. Shanghai is at the forefront of the trend. In any case, the Volunteer Army must develop a very good atmosphere. Not only must military training be disciplined and scientific, but also the character and conduct of soldiers must be upright, so as to become a model for the time and a permanent model for hundreds of years to come, leaving a foundation for future generations and others. Then, not only can Shanghai's school history occupy a place, but also Shanghai's city history can occupy a place. If we can do this, then Japan will never dare to invade our Northeast again. Even the shame accumulated over decades can be washed away in a short period of time.

▲Tao Baichuan's Speech Tao Baichuan, the oath supervisor of the Municipal Party Department, delivered a speech, stating that today, I am participating in this grand ceremony. In addition to wishing Director Wang and the Volunteer Army to achieve the goal of victory and success, I also have a small thought. Since China established the country thousands of years ago, it has always valued literature over military affairs. As the saying goes, what is gained on horseback cannot be governed on horseback. This means that the country that is not gained by military aggression cannot be governed by military force. Therefore, after the establishment of dynasties, it is necessary to stop military affairs and cultivate literature. There is also a common saying that good men do not become soldiers, and good iron is not used to make nails. This saying is even more common, and its meaning is even more obvious. It also says that others have swords, but I have pens like knives. This is enough to express our country's emphasis on literature over military affairs throughout history. Today, when foreign insults come, we adopt a policy of non-resistance, and internally, we cannot be peaceful. Internal and external pressure has created the modern social phenomenon of China. This cannot be said to be the result of valuing literature over military affairs. I remember that a Japanese scholar wrote a book called "On the Annexation of Manchuria and Mongolia," saying that there are two kinds of people in China, one is bandits, and the other is good people. All the scholars of Wenwu, Zhou Gong, Confucius, and Mencius are bandits, and the rest are good people. These good people are very indifferent to national ideology, so it doesn't matter if they are annexed. The only thing to fear is bandits. Modern bandits are young students. These people are quite fierce and have a deep understanding of national ideology and other issues. But fortunately, they can only do verbal and written propaganda and have no military force. We can conquer them by military force because these young people do not value military affairs but value literature. Therefore, it is okay to annex them. Therefore, Japan's four to fifty thousand troops can invade our China, and our China has more than two million troops, but they cannot resist Japan. Because the Japanese value military preparations, and every person has military training. If a formal war breaks out, then Japan's 60 million people are all troops, while our country's 400 million people still only have 2 million troops. It is painful to say this. This is why the Youth Volunteer Army must be organized and trained. In our old novels, it is often said that people have three heads and six arms. Now we already have two heads, namely, the pen and the tongue. If we can train the fist again, then we will have all three heads and will surely become a world power.

▲Chu Minyi's Speech Chu Minyi said that today is the day Director Wang takes office, and I feel that the spirit of the academic community is very scattered and must be united. Today's emphasis on literature over military affairs is an undeniable fact, but because the world is now a scientific world, guns and artillery are also based on literature. Literature studies science and then it occurs, so I hope that both literature and military affairs will be valued. Then Ms. Lin Kecong, a representative of the Women's Relief Association, and representatives of the military training department of various universities' anti-Japanese federations delivered speeches one after another.

▲Wang's Reply Director Wang replied that the oath supervisors, all the guests, and the representatives were all very sincere and sincerely accepted and deeply thanked for their kindness. Now, I will report on the training situation of the Volunteer Army: (1) Why was the military training office established? The Central Party Department, the Training Directorate, and the Ministry of Education consulted and believed that military training in various schools must have a responsible agency. Therefore, according to the promulgated guidelines for the implementation of the Volunteer Army, this office was established. (2) The motivation for organizing the Volunteer Army is to fight the violent Japanese with all our strength. (3) Training policy: (A) Do not hinder mine school administration (B) Respect student's will. There is a misunderstanding among people in society, that is, they think that the Volunteer Army is to fight the enemy with all their strength, which is a big mistake. The Volunteer Army is a student who has received many years of education and has rich scientific knowledge. Is it a pity to sacrifice on the battlefield as soldiers? Therefore, the Volunteer Army is the cadre to lead and train the rest of the people. Now some people are urging to issue guns. I think that the current problem of Volunteer Army training is an education problem, not a military problem. Basic knowledge must be done well before using guns. Therefore, it is not necessary to issue guns now. After the Volunteer Army is trained for six months, guns can be issued when they are trained again. It is also heard that Mr. Wang went to Beijing yesterday afternoon on the 4:30 express train to attend the Fourth National Congress and discuss military training matters.

A Record of Visiting Feng Yong 95

▲The Organization of the Northeast People's Group▲This Trip is Entirely Initiated by the People

▲Petitioning the Peace Conference Representatives Today▲The Agreed Scope Includes Four Points

Feng Yong, president of Feng Yong University, led a group of more than 600 people from the Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Group from Ping to Shanghai to petition the Beijing and Guangdong representatives of the Peace Conference. After arriving in Shanghai at 0:20 yesterday morning, because the Beijing and Guangdong representatives of the Peace Conference had come to a satisfactory end, it was decided that the entire group would go to the residences of the remaining Peace Representatives of both sides to petition this morning.

Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Group (Photo by this newspaper)

At about 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the team paraded around the Chinese community for a week and decided to go to Beijing tonight or tomorrow morning to petition the National Government. Yesterday, this reporter visited Feng in his hotel, Feng, wearing a western suit, overflowing with heroic spirit between his eyebrows, and chatting happily with the reporter, describing in detail the experience of being detained by the Japanese in Shenyang. He also said that the Northeast People's National Salvation Petition Group was entirely organized by the people of the Northeast, including faculty and students from Jilin, Northeast, Feng Yong, and Medical Universities, as well as staff from chambers of commerce and farmers' associations. I was temporarily elected as the commander-in-chief by the public before departure. I had no knowledge of the petition to the south beforehand. When the petition group was about to leave, Zhang Hanqing tried to dissuade them, fearing that it would cause misunderstandings in all parties, thinking that it was he who instigated it. After I strongly explained that this matter was entirely initiated by the people, please don't worry too much, and after repeated explanations, it was allowed to proceed. After arriving in Shanghai, the peace conference had come to an end. A general meeting was convened today to decide to go to the remaining peace representatives' offices in Shanghai to petition, and the scope of the petition was agreed upon, including four points: (1) Please report the process of the peace conference and the reasons for the conclusion; (2) Please indicate the foreign policy towards the Northeast decided in the peace conference and the countermeasures for Japan not withdrawing troops on the 16th, and future measures; (3) State the claims of the people of the Northeast; (4) Hope to complete unification as soon as possible and be consistent with foreign countries. It is planned to go to Beijing to petition the National Government tomorrow night or the day after tomorrow, and then return north. The reporter then asked what Mr. Feng thought of the fact that the Northeast authorities' non-resistance against Japan was deeply dissatisfied by the people of the country. Feng replied that he had made a detailed speech on this point at Peking University. I am absolutely not covering up Zhang Hanqing, but I deeply believe that this incident was caused by resistance on a daily basis. The so-called greatest resistance is the construction of railways such as the Jihai and Shenhai lines, and the creation of combined transportation to reduce freight rates, which has severely hit the South Manchuria Railway. Last year, the South Manchuria Railway laid off more than 1,000 employees due to poor business, and the loss reached 10 million yen, so they hated us deeply. Under accumulated grievances, this change occurred. If there had been no resistance on a daily basis and we had always relied on the Japanese, there would be no such thing today. Feng also said that the Northeast army is weaker in Black Province. The provincial defense army usually deploys four brigades. Two brigades were transferred into the customs during the campaign against Shi, so only two brigades remained in Black Province. The lack of supplies of ammunition and weapons, this time, the brave resistance against Japan is commendable. I believe that the Japanese army intends to extend its influence to the Taonan Road, and does not want to covet the capital of Heilongjiang Province so quickly.

Shao Lizi Returned to Beijing Last Night 96

▲Definitely Know That Huang Yingbai Did Not Leave Shanghai

▲Recalling the Conversation on the Morning of the 4th

Shao Lizi went to Beijing last night. When he left, he spoke with the reporter, generally as follows: (1) Recent rumors are very bizarre, such as saying that Mr. Huang Yingbai went to Japan to secretly negotiate, but I definitely know that Mr. Huang did not leave Shanghai. He gave a lecture at Jinan University a few days ago, and tomorrow (that is, today), Mr. Huang has decided to attend a memorial week speech somewhere. This rumor will be self-defeating. It is not surprising that Japanese newspapers publish such rumors, but it is a pity that newspapers run by our own people also attack their political enemies based on such unfounded rumors. It's too unpatriotic. (2) In recent days, one or two small newspapers have accused me of insulting reporters, with severe tone and expression, which is also very strange. When I arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 4th, a reporter asked how the future of peace was. I said that it was very optimistic. A reporter said that there was a rumor that the meeting was about to break down, was it true? I said that the meeting itself was never a problem. The atmosphere outside the meeting was not good because the newspapers published various excessive remarks during the talks. At that time, Mr. Wu Tiecheng was traveling with me and also said that if the newspapers could stop publishing such talks for a few days, peace could be achieved quickly. We all talked about it as a joke at the time, but a reporter wrote down Mr. Wu's words, saying that if the newspapers could stop publishing for a few days, it was a mishearing, and the small newspapers added embellishments, saying that I insulted the reporters. I never scold people, and everyone in the news media knows it. The reporter should also be able to recall whether my tone and expression were severe at that time.

General Assembly of Workers from Japanese Cotton Mills in Pudong 100

▲Over Seven Thousand Six Hundred People Attend

The Shanghai Municipal Japanese Cotton Mill Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held its second general assembly of workers from various Japanese cotton mills in Pudong at a movie theater at the end of Meizhou Road yesterday morning at 8:00 AM. Representatives from the Municipal Party Committee, Li Weixiong, the Social Affairs Bureau, Guo Yongxi, and the Postal Workers' Union, Liu Xinquan, Shui Xiangyun, and Dong Genfu, attended to provide guidance. Attending were all workers from the No. 2 Gonda Cotton Mill, the No. 2 Tongxing Cotton Mill, and worker representatives from the No. 1 Gonda Cotton Mill, the No. 2 and No. 3 Donghua Cotton Mills, the No. 1 and No. 2 Dakang Cotton Mills, and the No. 1, No. 2, No. 3, No. 4, and No. 5 Shanghai Cotton Mills, totaling over seven thousand six hundred people. The meeting agenda was as follows: (1) Publicly elected chairman: Cheng Deyuan; recorders: Hu Baiquan and Wei Shudong; (2) Formal ceremonies; (3) The chairman reported on the meeting's purpose and main points: (A) The association's and various parties' progress on arrangements and relief measures for workers after leaving the factories; (B) The Japanese government's attacks on our country this week; (C) The understanding and attitude that Japanese cotton mill workers should have; (4) The main points of the speech by representative Li from the Municipal Party Committee: (1) Eliminate five-minute enthusiasm; (2) Overthrow the comprador class of Japanese factories; (3) Abandon selfishness; (4) The speech by representative Liu from the Postal Workers' Union, "Why We Must Resist Japan and Save the Nation"; (5) Representatives from the No. 2 Gonda Cotton Mill, Huang Zihou, the No. 2 and No. 3 Shanghai Cotton Mills, Xing Agen and Zhao Dinghan, the No. 1 Shanghai Cotton Mill, Liu Jingqing, and the No. 2 Tongxing Cotton Mill, Yang Huaiyu, reported on the actual oppression of workers by the factory owners and the general situation of organizing workers to resist Japan; (6) The meeting adjourned. Subsequently, representatives from the No. 2 Gonda Cotton Mill, the No. 2 and No. 3 Shanghai Cotton Mills, the No. 1 Shanghai Cotton Mill, and the No. 2 Tongxing Cotton Mill went to the Pudong Office to hold separate representative meetings, elect key personnel in charge, and plan for next week's work. The executive committee members of the Japanese Cotton Mill Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, Cheng Deyuan, Wang Shoushan, Hu Baiquan, Hong Meipu, Bao Ziheng, Zhang Weisheng, and Wei Shudong, attended to provide guidance. The meetings adjourned at 3:00 PM.

The Seventh District Branch of the Municipal Federation Inspects Japanese Goods 101

The Japanese goods inspection team of the Seventh District Branch of the Citizens' Federation, led by Liu Zhongying, Zhou Fuzhang, Ouyang Biao, Pu Zhengtang, Zhou Lexiang, Jiang Jianpei, Fan Tianjin, Yan Zuqing, etc., inspected Japanese goods door-to-door along Broadway Road yesterday morning. Over fifty businesses were inspected, including Dou Chang Lianhao, Tongxing, Xinchengxing, Lihengchang, Hongxiang, Yijia Company, Zhu Yusheng, Wanjinji, Zhonghua, Meihua Company, Liang Tianxing, Xieshengchang, Fuan, Yuantai, Zhaoji, Futai, Zhenzhong Company, Yichangtai, Hengxingchang, Mu'ai Company, and Jingyi Company. After strict inspection, the following Japanese goods were sealed up: one large room of Ruichangtai Hardware, five rattan boxes of Quanji Black Embroidery Thread, two large rooms and eight boxes of Ruichangshun Hardware, five boxes and one cabinet of Yichang Hardware, eleven bundles of oil rope, four bundles of oil cups, two large rooms of Yichangsheng Hardware, one small package of Yangzhu from Chengchang Company, one box of Tongchang Hardware, four rooms of hardware sealed up by Zhengdaxiang, one bundle of Dayi Tinplate, two bundles and nineteen pieces of tin cans, three sets of Chengkang leather bag bead strings, one set of Yuji cigarette case cufflinks, one set of Zhenhua grass clips and beaded shoes, two sets of Xielong cigarette case leather wallets and cufflinks, one large room and thirteen boxes and nine pieces of Huafeng Hardware, one large room and five boxes of Ruixinshun Hardware, over seventy pieces of large and small Jinxiangxiang Hardware, twenty-four boxes of Gongxingchang Hardware, one large room of Ruichangtai Hardware, one large room of Hengdaxiang Hardware, one large room and six boxes of Qiantaixiang Hardware, six boxes of Yongchang Hardware, one cabinet of Yonghe Hardware, and one cabinet of Changji Hardware. These were immediately sealed up, and each business signed a pledge never to buy or sell Japanese goods again. It is reported that the team will continue to inspect door-to-door in the Tilanqiao area tomorrow to ensure a thorough cleanup.

Local News II

Murder Case of Mother and Daughter in Xiaonanmen 102

▲Motive Appears to be Robbery of Gold Jewelry▲Tragedy Arose from Cries for Help

At 3:30 PM yesterday, a robbery and murder case occurred at the intersection of Gujiading on Haichao Temple South Street, outside Xiaonanmen in Nanshi. Two people were shot and injured at the time. Passersby witnessed the scene and helped transport them to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. One of them died from severe injuries shortly after arriving at the hospital, while the other's injuries were also very critical. After investigation, it was determined that the two victims were a mother and daughter. The details are as follows:

▲The Ding Family, A Modest Family from Pudong. Qiu, the 54-year-old wife of Ding Maomao, a native of Pudong, has a daughter named Sanlang, who is 19 years old. The family of three lives at No. 3, Lane 346, near Guohuo Road in Nanshi. They make a living by growing vegetables. Because of their diligence and thrift, they have savings in addition to their monthly expenses, making them a modest family.

▲Robbery Interrupted. Yesterday after lunch, Qiu and her daughter went to Xiaodongmen to buy foreign cloth. They were returning around 3:00 PM when, as they passed the intersection of Gujiading on Haichao Temple South Street outside Xiaonanmen, two thugs suddenly appeared. Both were around 30 years old, dressed in blue cloth short shirts and pants, and spoke with a Jiangbei accent. They stopped them, displayed handguns, and forbade them from making any noise. Qiu and her daughter Sanlang knew they had encountered robbers and were terrified.

▲Cries for Help and Gunfire. The robbers immediately grabbed Sanlang's hand because she had a gold bracelet on her wrist and a gold ring on her finger. They forcefully removed the gold bracelet and were about to take off her gold ring and earrings when Qiu and her daughter, seeing the robbers forcibly taking their jewelry, resisted regardless of the consequences and cried out for help. Realizing the situation was unfavorable, the robbers suddenly fired two shots. Qiu and her daughter cried out in agony and immediately fell to the ground. The robbers, seeing that they had committed a bloody crime, immediately fled with the stolen gold bracelet, disappearing in an instant.

▲Wound Locations. After the robbers had fled, Qiu and her daughter, lying in pools of blood, were on the verge of death. Qiu was shot once in the left abdomen, and the bullet had not penetrated through. Her daughter Sanlang was wounded below her left breast, and the bullet exited through her back, the bright red blood flowing from the wound. Her pale face showed a deathly pallor, a truly unbearable sight. Passersby who witnessed the scene immediately transported the injured mother and daughter, along with two bundles of foreign cloth stained with blood, to Shanghai Hospital.

▲The Young Woman Dies. The daughter, Sanlang, died shortly after arriving at the hospital due to her severe injuries, without receiving any treatment. Her mother, Qiu, received emergency treatment from the doctors, who said that her injuries were severe and her life was in extreme danger. Her husband, Ding Maomao, rushed to the hospital upon hearing the news. He was overwhelmed with grief at the sight of his daughter's death and his wife's injuries, nearly collapsing from sorrow.

▲Rumored Cause. It is rumored that Qiu and her daughter decorated themselves lavishly when they went out to buy foreign cloth. They were noticed by the robbers as they bought the cloth and returned from Xiaodongmen Street. The two robbers followed them to Gujiading, where the area was very secluded, and then they acted. Unexpectedly, the mother and daughter resisted the robbers to protect their beloved gold jewelry, which resulted in their injuries and death. Alas, how pitiful!

Total Amount of Seawall Projects in Tanggong 103

▲Totaling Over 1.3 Million Yuan▲Submitted to Provincial Authorities for Approval

Since taking office, Director Shen of the Baoshan Jiangnan Seawall Works Office has estimated the total cost of the seawall projects in Baoshan, Songjiang, Taicang, and Changshu counties. The project for Baoshan, spanning over 2,000 zhang, is estimated to cost 700,000 yuan for labor and materials; Songjiang, over 400 zhang, about 200,000 yuan; Taicang, over 900 zhang, about 250,000 yuan; and Changshu, over 140 zhang, about 20,000 yuan, totaling over 1.3 million yuan. The project has been submitted to the provincial authorities for approval, and construction will begin soon.

Emergency Meeting of Journalists' Association Yesterday 104

▲Shishi Xinbao Newspaper Agrees to the Last Demands of the Association Members

▲General Assembly to be Held on Wednesday to Discuss Reorganization into a Guild

The Shanghai Journalists' Association held a temporary emergency general assembly yesterday at 3:00 PM at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce regarding the layoffs at the Shishi Xinbao Newspaper. Over a hundred people attended. Hang Shijun, Jiang Jianhou, and Tang Demin were publicly elected as chairmen, and Xu Chichen served as recorder. After the formal ceremonies, Hang Shijun delivered the opening remarks. Jiang Xiangqing, a representative of the Shishi Xinbao Newspaper Association, reported on the layoffs. Guanghua Bookstore Accused of Forging Seals and Infringing Copyright 106

▲Problem Arises with the Book "China Under Economic Aggression"

Qi Ling, a woman from Sichuan, previously entrusted Guanghua Bookstore on Fuzhou Road to publish her late husband Qi Shufen's book "China Under Economic Aggression." According to the contract, each edition was limited to 1,000 copies, and they could only be sold after being stamped by Liu Zemin. So far, eight editions have been published. Recently, Liu saw the book being sold by the bookstore and, although it was stamped, it was definitely not the stamp he had used. He informed the copyright owner, Qi Ling, who negotiated with Guanghua Bookstore but failed to reach a satisfactory resolution. Qi then filed a criminal complaint against Guanghua in the First Special District Court, accusing them of forging seals and infringing copyright. The court accepted the complaint and has notified the defendant to await a scheduled hearing.

Liu Tingshi Accused of Forcibly Defiling His Fiancée 107

▲Change of Heart After Establishing a Relationship▲Refusing to Marry Her▲Parents-in-Law File a Lawsuit

Liu Tingshi (also known as Xi San) and his wife Luo Mengbi, residents of No. 475, Lianbao Lane, Kangnaot Road, West Shanghai, recently filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Court, accusing their prospective son-in-law, Wang Xianggu, of the crimes of rape and abduction. They requested that he be punished according to Articles 257, Section 2, and 240, Section 1, of the Criminal Law and, in an attached civil lawsuit, requested damages of 30,000 yuan in accordance with Articles 184 and 195 of the Civil Law. The main points of their lawsuit are as follows: The defendant, Wang Xianggu, used to run a business in Yichang and had considerable influence. He was once the chairman of the Yichang Chamber of Commerce and was a member of the upper class. The plaintiff, Liu, had served as an official in Yichang twice, and that is how he came to know Wang. The plaintiff's only daughter, Liu Can (also known as Wenjin), 19 years old, also went to Yichang. Wang then asked someone to propose marriage. The plaintiff, considering him to be a businessman of the upper class, agreed. Later, the plaintiff retired and came to Shanghai, and Wang soon came to Shanghai as well. He often visited the plaintiff's home, and he and Liu Can often met. Then, on December 14th of last year, Liu Can suddenly disappeared without a trace. On the 18th, Liu Tingshi suddenly received a letter by airmail. Upon opening it, he learned that it was a letter from his beloved daughter from Hankou, stating that the defendant had tricked her into going to Hankou and raped her. After Wang achieved his purpose of defiling her, he abandoned her in an inn, disregarding everything. She asked him to come and rescue her immediately. Luo Mengbi, her mother, went to Hankou, found her daughter, and negotiated with Wang Xianggu, ordering him to marry her immediately. The wedding could take place in Yichang or Shanghai, but Wang refused. Therefore, Liu filed a lawsuit. The court approved the petition and issued a summons. However, the whereabouts of the defendant, Wang Xianggu, were unknown. Therefore, he ordered the plaintiff, Liu Tingshi, to accompany the Chinese constable Jin Wanrong, who was responsible for delivering the summons, and scheduled the trial for the 15th.

Tailor A Jin Dies of Cholera 108

▲At the Zhujing Team Headquarters

Xu A Jin, a false regiment commander and subordinate of the lake bandit Tai Bao A Shu, also known as Tailor A Jin, was hiding in Shanghai. Water Police Captain Fan arrested him at a small restaurant in South Shanghai and brought him back to the Zhujing team headquarters for interrogation and detention. Unexpectedly, the bandit Xu suddenly died of acute cholera in the detention center the day before yesterday. Captain Fan has reported this to the district headquarters and the Jinshan County Government, and officials have been sent to Zhujing to confirm the cause of death and prepare a coffin for burial.

Zhejiang Province to Extradite Wu Tianbao 109

The notorious bandit leader Wu Tianbao (nicknamed Mud Carpenter A Bao) committed crimes in Zhejiang, fled to Shanghai, and opened fire to resist arrest, killing Detective Jiang Yunzhong. He was later captured by a French Concession detective and sent to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention. The Zhejiang Security Office received news of this and yesterday sent Special Agent Wang and four soldiers from Hangzhou by train to Shanghai. They are prepared to submit a request to the Second Special District Court today for extradition so that the bandit leader can be brought back to Hangzhou to be investigated and prosecuted.

Robbery and Shooting of Pedestrians 110

Wang Zizhong, a 29-year-old Cantonese man, has been running the Heli Pottery Shop at No. 33, Laobeimen Street, French Concession, for over ten years. Because the location is in a strategic area, business is exceptionally prosperous. At 9:05 PM last night, as the shop's accountant was sorting out the accounts, three robbers suddenly appeared, one wearing a gray Western suit and two wearing long robes, each armed with a handgun. They rushed into the shop, forbade anyone from making a sound, and drove all the employees to a corner. They then robbed approximately 80 yuan in cash and coins from the counter and fled south towards Minquan Road. The employees immediately gave chase, shouting "Catch the robbers!" along the way. One robber immediately turned around and fired two shots, and a passerby fell to the ground. The robbers took the opportunity to escape without a trace. Nearby detectives also rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm and found a man around 30 years old, wearing a gabardine jacket, felt hat, and Zhigong cloth shoes, shot in the left chest. He was still able to speak and said his name was Lu Mingzhang and he worked as a salesman at the Sun Guangxing Watch Shop on Wuma Road. After speaking, his face turned pale, and he soon died. Next to him were an invoice and three new watches. The detectives then took the shop owner to the police station to report the incident, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Mortuary to be examined, and the court was notified.

First Sending Fecal Matter, Then Throwing Intimidation Letters 112

▲Seeking Revenge for Debt Disputes▲Strange Odor in the New House

Hu Kun, also known as Qianzi Monk, a local resident of No. 39, Cunren Lane, Baoshan Road, is currently a guard team director. He was once a poor man but has accumulated wealth in recent years. He lends money and collects interest, and has become a well-off household, buying land and building a house. Due to debt collection, he is resented by others. On the 6th of this month, several people sent two wine jars, claiming they were gifts, and immediately opened them, unexpectedly filling the house with fecal matter. The senders fled, leaving the new house filled with the smell. Hu could only complain in vain. Then, on the afternoon of the 7th, he suddenly received an intimidation letter, stating that he was a rich man and ordering him to send 2,000 yuan to the Qingyun Road Bridge within five days, dressed in a bamboo cloth long shirt, wearing a white-topped hat, and carrying a small vegetable scale as a sign. If he did not send the money, he would be "eating health pills." Hu was terrified and has reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau, requesting protection.

General Assembly of Representatives from Japanese Cotton Mills in West Shanghai 115

Yesterday morning at around 10:00 AM, representatives from all Japanese cotton mill workers in West Shanghai held a general assembly at the West Shanghai Commune. Over three hundred people attended, including representatives from the Municipal Party Committee, Lu Jingshi, and representatives from the Postal Workers' Union Anti-Japanese Association, Yu Songqiao and Tu Heyun. Gu Ruhang was publicly elected as chairman. After the formal ceremonies, Chairman Gu reported that the atrocities of the Japanese were outrageous and that failure to resist with force would be a sign of national demise. He said that the patriotic enthusiasm of male and female compatriots serving in Japanese cotton mills was second to none, but that due to the severe droughts and floods, withdrawing from Japanese factories en masse might lead to loss of livelihood, hunger, and cold. The chairman understood their difficulties and was requesting various Chinese commercial factories to make proper arrangements for them and hoped that all workers would wait until the League of Nations' deadline of November 16th to decide whether to stay or leave. He said that the country was in dire straits and that they should not be incited. His speech was deeply moving, and the representatives of the workers were all moved to tears. Because the meeting place was small and the number of people was too large, the Municipal Health Bureau sent a mobile ambulance to the scene in case of emergency.

Three cotton mill workers, Song Shaoji, etc., were previously beaten and injured by Japanese on Macao Road. The District Court sentenced the perpetrators to a fine of three yuan. Yu Binqi Seeks Clarification from the Anti-Japanese Association 118

Yu Binqi, the inventor of the Chinese typewriter, copper traveling pillow, and ingenious printing machine, was extremely angered by yesterday's newspaper report stating that the Chinese typewriter was a Japanese product disguised as a domestic product. Yesterday, he personally went to the Anti-Japanese Association to clarify, stating that since the Manchurian Incident, the Chinese typewriter had been repeatedly investigated by members of your association. He had shown the manufacturing factory and order receipts from various domestic factories to the public. If the association still did not believe him, it would leave the common people with no place to seek redress. He now made an agreement with your association that if, within three days, it was found that the Chinese typewriter had purchased parts from Japan or requested Japanese labor for its engineering since the outbreak of the Northeast Incident, Binqi would die in front of the public to demonstrate the consequences of being a traitorous merchant and to demonstrate your association's patriotic enthusiasm. Otherwise, he asked how your association would handle the matter and requested it to be made public.

Third District Party Headquarters Reprints and Distributes "Japanese Conspiracy and Atrocities Against China" 121

In order to expand anti-Japanese propaganda, the Third District Party Headquarters of this city has compiled a book titled "Japanese Conspiracy and Atrocities Against China" based on true and reliable evidence of Japanese conspiracies and atrocities against China. Its contents include "An Overview of the China Policy of the Two Major Political Parties in Japan," "Japan's War Plan Against China," "Japan's Economic Aggression Policy Against China," "An Outline of the Tanaka Cabinet's Active Policy Towards Manchuria and Mongolia," "A Summary of Unequal Treaties Between China and Japan," "A Glimpse of Japan's Invasion of Manchuria," "Translated Highlights of Japan's Secret Meeting on Maintaining Rights and Interests in Manchuria and Mongolia," and "Statistics on Japanese Atrocities in China Since the First Year of the Republic." The book contains more than 100,000 words and is based on reliable evidence. The first printing of 5,000 copies was distributed to all sectors, and they were all claimed in a few days. The second edition was printed yesterday, and people from all walks of life can go to claim copies.

Li Guozhen Comes to Shanghai to Report on His Legal Practice 122

Mr. Li Guozhen, a member of the Jiangxi Provincial Assembly in the First National Assembly, graduated from the Department of Political Science at Waseda University in Japan. Since the early years of the Republic, he served as a member of the Provisional Senate, where his eloquence caused a sensation. Every time he took the stage, the audience was packed, and both Chinese and foreign people praised him. In the election for the First National Assembly, he was re-elected. After the dissolution of the National Assembly in the Gui Chou year, the government specially sent him to England, Germany, France, Italy, and other countries to study politics. After returning to China, he held important positions and maintained integrity. Since the twelfth year of the Republic, he resigned in anger due to Cao's bribery and closed his doors to retreat, focusing on writing and studying law. Now, he has come to Shanghai from Beiping, renting an apartment on the upper floor of the Shanghai Silk Company at 656 Jing'an Temple Road, engaging in legal practice. Many prominent figures in the local banking and industrial sectors are old friends of Mr. Li and have been hosting banquets to welcome him. There is a great deal of social activity. It is said that the legal profession here has gained another strong general.

The monthly magazine "Education and the People" is published on a regular basis by the Research and Experiment Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute of Wuxi. Shanghai Citizens Promoting Domestic Goods Association Certifies Dahua Lake Crepe 126

The Shanghai Citizens Promoting Domestic Goods Association certified that Dahua Lake Crepe, produced by Dahua Industrial Factory and sold in Xiamen, was suspected of being a Japanese product by the Anti-Japanese Association there due to its excellent quality and was detained for verification. The association sent a letter of certification, which read: "To the Xiamen Anti-Japanese Association, Regarding the letter from member Dahua Industrial Factory stating that member's product Dahua Lake Crepe, i.e. Jinwen Crepe, was sold in Xiamen and a misunderstanding occurred, please provide certification. After investigation, the factory is entirely Chinese-owned and the product is a second-class domestic product according to the national product standards promulgated by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce. When it joined our association as a factory member in the 17th year of the Republic of China, the investigation department sent personnel to investigate and verify that the product was genuine. It was resolved at the 22nd meeting of the 11th session of the Standing Committee to provide certification on record. Accordingly, we send a special letter of certification, hoping that your association will maintain it to facilitate sales, and we will appreciate your public-spiritedness."

Grand Theatre. Tickets have already gone on sale through the Motley Company. Music lovers will be able to feast their ears at that time.

Compilation and Printing of "Compendium of Japanese Trademarks" 129

Since the Japanese army occupied the Northeast, compatriots across the country have been striving for the anti-Japanese national salvation movement, with economic severance from Japan being the only anti-Japanese vanguard. However, inspections of Japanese goods in various places often lead to misunderstandings due to the inability to distinguish them in detail. The International Commercial Research Institute is compiling and printing a large volume of "Compendium of Japanese Trademarks," which will categorize and reproduce all kinds of Japanese goods trademarks on copper plates. It is exquisitely printed on Jiangnan Lianshi paper and is about two hundred pages thick. It also includes a title by Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, and prefaces by Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and Yan Esheng, Secretary-General of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. It is currently being rushed into printing and is expected to be published by the end of this month. The general distributor is Xinsheng News Agency, Daxin Square, 49 Hankou Road.

▲ The New-Style Laundry Industry Association, in April of this year, when the Stamp Tax Bureau sent personnel to inspect the stamps, took away the number slips used by the industry to give to customers with the intention of imposing a fine. This aroused public anger among the industry. A temporary meeting of all member representatives was convened, and it was discussed that this number slip was different in nature from an invoice. The stub had already been affixed with a stamp, and the slip was originally intended to facilitate customer procedures temporarily and was still to be retrieved. How could it be regarded as the same? It was resolved to submit it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and request the Stamp Tax Bureau to allow exemption from affixing stamps in order to relieve business difficulties. The matter was pending for a long time. In the past month, a letter was received from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that stamp inspection would begin on the first of this month. The matter was immediately submitted to the executive committee for discussion, and a re-petition was submitted. It was difficult to agree to the matter before a resolution was reached. Later, a letter was received from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that the request was not approved and that stamps had to be affixed. A temporary emergency meeting was convened yesterday, and it was resolved to organize a Stamp Tax Petition Committee, with Luo Zheng, Sun Jiangzuo, Lin Zhikun, Chen Shouzhi, and Huang Shoucheng elected as members. It was also submitted to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to be forwarded to the Stamp Tax Bureau, requesting temporary exemption from fines during the petition period. On the one hand, all members were notified to continue to affix stamps worth one cent as before and wait for a resolution.

Weather Report 137

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather in the Yangtze River basin was sunny and mild, with fog in the morning. There was a southwest wind in the Yellow Sea, and the wind in the East China Sea was non-directional. The weather in southern Taiwan and the Dongsha Islands was extremely bad due to a hurricane moving northwest. The center of the hurricane was within 60 miles of the intersection of 17 degrees north latitude and 119 degrees east longitude at approximately 11:00 AM. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 72.0 degrees and the lowest was 45.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 63.7 degrees and the lowest was 50.1 degrees.

To the Editor,

Upon reading your newspaper's local news column on the 4th of this month, I was startled to see my humble name listed among the party members in the telegram to Wang and Cai. Since October 26th, I have been engaged in propaganda in various villages with the anti-Japanese national salvation rural mobile propaganda team, and only returned to Qingpu on the 5th of this month. I had no prior knowledge of this telegram. Furthermore, it is incomprehensible that the names of Chen Kui and Guo Gen, who are not party members in the entire Qingpu County, were included in the telegram at the same time. Fearing that outsiders may misunderstand, I specially write this letter to clarify the matter. I earnestly request that you promptly publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column to reveal the truth. I am deeply grateful. Respectfully submitted to the esteemed editor of Shen Bao, Guo Qinfu, party member of Qingpu County, November 7th.
